		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidip-03.nroff') !== '0e3d85279f55f519ca327a3a7b0ec2935e799bb3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidip-03.nroff');
		}
	}
}
